# Prometheus prometheus-common HTTP Config to TLS Chain

## Your Task

Trace how TLS configuration flows from prometheus/prometheus through prometheus-common to the actual tls.Config used in HTTP clients. Find Go source files in both repos that define, validate, and apply TLSConfig for scrape and remote-write HTTP connections.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
*(none — all repos available locally)*

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

  1128→type TLSConfigOption interface {
  1129→	applyToTLSConfigOptions(options *tlsConfigOptions)
  1130→}
  1131→
  1132→// NewTLSConfig creates a new tls.Config from the given TLSConfig.
  1133→func NewTLSConfig(cfg *TLSConfig, optFuncs ...TLSConfigOption) (*tls.Config, error) {
  1134→	return NewTLSConfigWithContext(context.Background(), cfg, optFuncs...)
  1135→}
  1136→
  1137→// NewTLSConfigWithContext creates a new tls.Config from the given TLSConfig.
  1138→func NewTLSConfigWithContext(ctx context.Context, cfg *TLSConfig, optFuncs ...TLSConfigOption) (*tls.Config, error) {
  1139→	opts := tlsConfigOptions{}
  1140→	for _, opt := range optFuncs {
  1141→		opt.applyToTLSConfigOptions(&opts)
  1142→	}
  1143→
  1144→	if err := cfg.Validate(); err != nil {
  1145→		return nil, err
  1146→	}
  1147→
  1148→	tlsConfig := &tls.Config{
  1149→		InsecureSkipVerify: cfg.InsecureSkipVerify,
  1150→		MinVersion:         uint16(cfg.MinVersion),
  1151→		MaxVersion:         uint16(cfg.MaxVersion),
  1152→	}
  1153→
  1154→	if cfg.MaxVersion != 0 && cfg.MinVersion != 0 {
  1155→		if cfg.MaxVersion < cfg.MinVersion {
  1156→			return nil, errors.New("tls_config.max_version must be greater than or equal to tls_config.min_version if both are specified")
  1157→		}
  1158→	}
  1159→
  1160→	// If a CA cert is provided then let's read it in so we can validate the
  1161→	// scrape target's certificate properly.
  1162→	caSecret, err := toSecret(opts.secretManager, Secret(cfg.CA), cfg.CAFile, cfg.CARef)
  1163→	if err != nil {
  1164→		return nil, fmt.Errorf("unable to use CA cert: %w", err)
  1165→	}
  1166→	if caSecret != nil {
  1167→		ca, err := caSecret.Fetch(ctx)
  1168→		if err != nil {
  1169→			return nil, fmt.Errorf("unable to read CA cert: %w", err)
  1170→		}
  1171→		i

  1302→func (c *TLSConfig) getClientCertificate(ctx context.Context, secretManager SecretManager) (*tls.Certificate, error) {
  1303→	var (
  1304→		certData, keyData string
  1305→		err               error
  1306→	)
  1307→
  1308→	certSecret, err := toSecret(secretManager, Secret(c.Cert), c.CertFile, c.CertRef)
  1309→	if err != nil {
  1310→		return nil, fmt.Errorf("unable to use client cert: %w", err)
  1311→	}
  1312→	if certSecret != nil {
  1313→		certData, err = certSecret.Fetch(ctx)
  1314→		if err != nil {
  1315→			return nil, fmt.Errorf("unable to read specified client cert: %w", err)
  1316→		}
  1317→	}
  1318→
  1319→	keySecret, err := toSecret(secretManager, c.Key, c.KeyFile, c.KeyRef)
  1320→	if err != nil {
  1321→		return nil, fmt.Errorf("unable to use client key: %w", err)
  1322→	}
  1323→	if keySecret != nil {
  1324→		keyData, err = keySecret.Fetch(ctx)
  1325→		if err != nil {
  1326→			return nil, fmt.Errorf("unable to read specified client key: %w", err)
  1327→		}
  1328→	}
  1329→
  1330→	cert, err := tls.X509KeyPair([]byte(certData), []byte(keyData))
  1331→	if err != nil {
  1332→		return nil, fmt.Errorf("unable to use specified client cert (%s) & key (%s): %w", certSecret.Description(), keySecret.Description(), err)
  1333→	}
  1334→
  1335→	return &cert, nil
  1336→}
  1337→
  1338→// updateRootCA parses the given byte slice as a series of PEM encoded certificates and updates tls.Config.RootCAs.
  1339→func updateRootCA(cfg *tls.Config, b []byte) bool {
  1340→	caCertPool := x509.NewCertPool()
  1341→	if !caCertPool.AppendCertsFromPEM(b) {
  1342→		return false
  1343→	}
  1344→	cfg.RootCAs = caCertPool
  1345→	return true
  1346→}

    32→// LoadTLSConfig parses the given file into a tls.Config.
    33→func LoadTLSConfig(filename string) (*tls.Config, error) {
    34→	content, err := os.ReadFile(filename)
    35→	if err != nil {
    36→		return nil, err
    37→	}
    38→	cfg := TLSConfig{}
    39→	switch filepath.Ext(filename) {
    40→	case ".yml":
    41→		if err = yaml.UnmarshalStrict(content, &cfg); err != nil {
    42→			return nil, err
    43→		}
    44→	case ".json":
    45→		decoder := json.NewDecoder(bytes.NewReader(content))
    46→		decoder.DisallowUnknownFields()
    47→		if err = decoder.Decode(&cfg); err != nil {
    48→			return nil, err
    49→		}
    50→	default:
    51→		return nil, fmt.Errorf("Unknown extension: %s", filepath.Ext(filename))
    52→	}
    53→	return NewTLSConfig(&cfg)

Perfect! I've successfully created a comprehensive analysis of the TLS configuration flow in the Prometheus ecosystem. Here's a summary of what I've documented:

## Summary

I've traced the complete TLS configuration chain from **prometheus/prometheus** through **prometheus/common** to the actual `crypto/tls.Config` used in HTTP clients. The analysis includes:

### Key Findings:

1. **Configuration Definition** (prometheus/prometheus):
   - `ScrapeConfig` and `RemoteWriteConfig` embed `HTTPClientConfig` 
   - These define how scrape targets and remote-write endpoints are accessed

2. **Core TLS Implementation** (prometheus/common):
   - `TLSConfig` struct encapsulates certificate paths, inline certs, and TLS version constraints
   - Supports three sources: files, inline values, and secret manager references
   - Includes validation and YAML unmarshaling

3. **Client Creation Pipeline**:
   - Entry points: `newScrapeClient()` (scrape), `NewReadClient()` / `NewWriteClient()` (remote storage)
   - `NewClientFromConfig()` → `NewRoundTripperFromConfigWithContext()` → `NewTLSConfigWithContext()`
   - Final `tls.Config` is embedded in `http.Transport.TLSClientConfig`

4. **Dynamic Reloading**:
   - `NewTLSRoundTripperWithContext()` watches certificate file hashes
   - Automatically reloads certificates when files change
   - Handles CA cert updates and client certificate rotation

5. **Certificate Handling**:
   - `updateRootCA()` parses PEM certificates and populates `tls.Config.RootCAs`
   - `getClientCertificate()` creates `tls.X509KeyPair` from cert+key pairs
   - Supports both client authentication and server certificate validation

The answer has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json` with complete file listings, symbol definitions, and the execution chain.

the host header.\nfunc WithHost(host string) HTTPClientOption {\n\treturn httpClientOptionFunc(func(opts *httpClientOptions) {\n\t\topts.host = host\n\t})\n}\n\ntype secretManagerOption struct &secretManagerOption{\n\t\tsecretManager: manager,\n\t}\n}\n\n// NewClient returns a http.Client using the specified http.RoundTripper.\nfunc newClient(rt http.RoundTripper) *http.Client {\n\treturn &http.Client{Transport: rt}\n}\n\n// NewClientFromConfig returns a new HTTP client configured for the\n// given config.HTTPClientConfig and config.HTTPClientOption.\n// The name is used as go-conntrack metric label.\nfunc NewClientFromConfig(cfg HTTPClientConfig, name string, optFuncs ...HTTPClientOption) (*http.Client, error) {\n\trt, err := NewRoundTripperFromConfig(cfg, name, optFuncs...)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tclient := newClient(rt)\n\tif !cfg.FollowRedirects {\n\t\tclient.CheckRedirect = func(*http.Request, []*http.Request) error {\n\t\t\treturn {\n\treturn NewRoundTripperFromConfigWithContext(context.Background(), cfg, name, optFuncs...)\n}\n\n// NewRoundTripperFromConfigWithContext returns a new HTTP RoundTripper configured for the\n// given config.HTTPClientConfig and config.HTTPClientOption.\n// The name is used as go-conntrack metric label.\nfunc NewRoundTripperFromConfigWithContext(ctx context.Context, cfg HTTPClientConfig, name string, optFuncs ...HTTPClientOption) (http.RoundTripper, error) {\n\topts := defaultHTTPClientOptions\n\tfor _, opt := range optFuncs {\n\t\topt.applyToHTTPClientOptions(&opts)\n\t}\n\n\tvar dialContext func(ctx context.Context, network, addr string) (net.Conn, error)\n\n\tif opts.dialContextFunc != nil {\n\t\tdialContext = conntrack.NewDialContextFunc(\n\t\t\tconntrack.DialWithDialContextFunc((func(context.Context, string, string) (net.Conn, error))(opts.dialContextFunc)),\n\t\t\tconntrack.DialWithTracing(),\n\t\t\tconntrack.DialWithName(name))\n\t} else {\n\t\tdialContext = conntrack.NewDialContextFunc(\n\t\t\tconntrack.DialWithTracing(),\n\t\t\tconntrack.DialWithName(name))\n\t}\n\n\tnewRT := func(tlsConfig *tls.Config) (http.RoundTripper, error) {\n\t\t// The only timeout we care about is the configured scrape timeout.\n\t\t// It is applied on request. So we leave out any timings here.\n\t\tvar rt http.RoundTripper = &http.Transport{\n\t\t\tProxy:                 cfg.Proxy(),\n\t\t\tProxyConnectHeader:    cfg.GetProxyConnectHeader(),\n\t\t\tMaxIdleConns:          20000,\n\t\t\tMaxIdleConnsPerHost:   1000, // see https://github.com/golang/go/issues/13801\n\t\t\tDisableKeepAlives:     !opts.keepAlivesEnabled,\n\t\t\tTLSClientConfig:       tlsConfig,\n\t\t\tDisableCompression:    true,\n\t\t\tIdleConnTimeout:       opts.idleConnTimeout,\n\t\t\tTLSHandshakeTimeout:   10 * time.Second,\n\t\t\tExpectContinueTimeout: 1 * time.Second,\n\t\t\tDialContext:           dialContext,\n\t\t}\n\t\tif opts.http2Enabled && cfg.EnableHTTP2 {\n\t\t\thttp2t, err := http2.ConfigureTransports(rt.(*http.Transport))\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\thttp2t.ReadIdleTimeout = time.Minute\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If a authorization_credentials is provided, create a round tripper that will set the\n\t\t// Authorization header correctly on each request.\n\t\tif cfg.Authorization != nil {\n\t\t\tcredentialsSecret, err := toSecret(opts.secretManager, cfg.Authorization.Credentials, cfg.Authorization.CredentialsFile, cfg.Authorization.CredentialsRef)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use credentials: %w\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trt = NewAuthorizationCredentialsRoundTripper(cfg.Authorization.Type, credentialsSecret, rt)\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Backwards compatibility, be nice with importers who would not have\n\t\t// called Validate().\n\t\tif len(cfg.BearerToken) > 0 || len(cfg.BearerTokenFile) > 0 {\n\t\t\tbearerSecret, err := toSecret(opts.secretManager, cfg.BearerToken, cfg.BearerTokenFile, \"\")\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use bearer token: %w\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trt = NewAuthorizationCredentialsRoundTripper(\"Bearer\", bearerSecret, rt)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif cfg.BasicAuth != nil {\n\t\t\tusernameSecret, err := toSecret(opts.secretManager, Secret(cfg.BasicAuth.Username), cfg.BasicAuth.UsernameFile, cfg.BasicAuth.UsernameRef)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use username: %w\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tpasswordSecret, err := toSecret(opts.secretManager, cfg.BasicAuth.Password, cfg.BasicAuth.PasswordFile, cfg.BasicAuth.PasswordRef)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use password: %w\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trt = NewBasicAuthRoundTripper(usernameSecret, passwordSecret, rt)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif cfg.OAuth2 != nil {\n\t\t\tvar (\n\t\t\t\toauthCredential SecretReader\n\t\t\t\terr             error\n\t\t\t)\n\n\t\t\tif cfg.OAuth2.GrantType == grantTypeJWTBearer {\n\t\t\t\toauthCredential, err = toSecret(opts.secretManager, cfg.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKey, cfg.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKeyFile, cfg.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKeyRef)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use client certificate: %w\", err)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\toauthCredential, err = toSecret(opts.secretManager, cfg.OAuth2.ClientSecret, cfg.OAuth2.ClientSecretFile, cfg.OAuth2.ClientSecretRef)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to use client secret: %w\", err)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trt = NewOAuth2RoundTripper(oauthCredential, cfg.OAuth2, rt, &opts)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif cfg.HTTPHeaders != nil {\n\t\t\trt = NewHeadersRoundTripper(cfg.HTTPHeaders, rt)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif opts.userAgent != \"\" {\n\t\t\trt = NewUserAgentRoundTripper(opts.userAgent, rt)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif opts.host != \"\" {\n\t\t\trt = NewHostRoundTripper(opts.host, rt)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Return a new configured RoundTripper.\n\t\treturn rt, nil\n\t}\n\n\ttlsConfig, err := opts.newTLSConfigFunc(ctx, &cfg.TLSConfig, WithSecretManager(opts.secretManager))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\ttlsSettings, err := cfg.TLSConfig.roundTripperSettings(opts.secretManager)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tif tlsSettings.immutable() {\n\t\t// No need for a RoundTripper that reloads the files automatically.\n\t\treturn newRT(tlsConfig)\n\t}\n\treturn NewTLSRoundTripperWithContext(ctx, tlsConfig, tlsSettings, newRT)\n}\n\n// SecretManager manages secret data mapped to names known as \"references\" or \"refs\".\ntype SecretManager interface {\n\t// Fetch returns the secret data given a secret name indicated by `secretRef`.\n\tFetch(ctx context.Context, secretRef string) (string, error)\n}\n\ntype SecretReader interface {\n\tFetch(ctx context.Context) (string, error)\n\tDescription() string\n\tImmutable() bool\n}\n\ntype InlineSecret struct {\n\ttext string\n}\n\nfunc NewInlineSecret(text string) *InlineSecret {\n\treturn &InlineSecret{text: text}\n}\n\nfunc (s *InlineSecret) Fetch(context.Context) (string, error) {\n\treturn s.text, nil\n}\n\nfunc (*InlineSecret) Description() string {\n\treturn \"inline\"\n}\n\nfunc (*InlineSecret) Immutable() bool {\n\treturn true\n}\n\ntype FileSecret struct {\n\tfile string\n}\n\nfunc NewFileSecret(file string) *FileSecret {\n\treturn &FileSecret{file: file}\n}\n\nfunc (s *FileSecret) Fetch(context.Context) (string, error) {\n\tfileBytes, err := os.ReadFile(s.file)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn \"\", fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read file %s: %w\", s.file, err)\n\t}\n\treturn strings.TrimSpace(string(fileBytes)), nil\n}\n\nfunc (s *FileSecret) Description() string {\n\treturn \"file \" + s.file\n}\n\nfunc (*FileSecret) Immutable() bool {\n\treturn false\n}\n\n// refSecret fetches a single secret from a SecretManager.\ntype refSecret struct {\n\tref     string\n\tmanager SecretManager // manager is expected to be not nil.\n}\n\nfunc (s *refSecret) Fetch(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {\n\treturn s.manager.Fetch(ctx, s.ref)\n}\n\nfunc (s *refSecret) Description() string {\n\treturn \"ref \" + s.ref\n}\n\nfunc (*refSecret) Immutable() bool {\n\treturn false\n}\n\n// toSecret returns a SecretReader from one of the given sources, assuming exactly\n// one or none of the sources are provided.\nfunc toSecret(secretManager SecretManager, text Secret, file, ref string) (SecretReader, error) {\n\tif text != \"\" {\n\t\treturn NewInlineSecret(string(text)), nil\n\t}\n\tif file != \"\" {\n\t\treturn NewFileSecret(file), nil\n\t}\n\tif ref != \"\" {\n\t\tif secretManager == nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"cannot use secret ref without manager\")\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn &refSecret{\n\t\t\tref:     ref,\n\t\t\tmanager: secretManager,\n\t\t}, nil\n\t}\n\treturn nil, nil\n}\n\ntype authorizationCredentialsRoundTripper struct {\n\tauthType        string\n\tauthCredentials SecretReader\n\trt              http.RoundTripper\n}\n\n// NewAuthorizationCredentialsRoundTripper adds the authorization credentials\n// read from the provided SecretReader to a request unless the authorization header\n// has already been set.\nfunc NewAuthorizationCredentialsRoundTripper(authType string, authCredentials SecretReader, rt http.RoundTripper) http.RoundTripper {\n\treturn &authorizationCredentialsRoundTripper{authType, authCredentials, rt}\n}\n\nfunc (rt *authorizationCredentialsRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n\tif len(req.Header.Get(\"Authorization\")) != 0 {\n\t\treturn rt.rt.RoundTrip(req)\n\t}\n\n\tvar authCredentials string\n\tif rt.authCredentials != nil {\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\tauthCredentials, err = rt.authCredentials.Fetch(req.Context())\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read authorization credentials: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treq = cloneRequest(req)\n\treq.Header.Set(\"Authorization\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%s %s\", rt.authType, authCredentials))\n\n\treturn rt.rt.RoundTrip(req)\n}\n\nfunc (rt *authorizationCredentialsRoundTripper) CloseIdleConnections() {\n\tif ci, ok := rt.rt.(closeIdler); ok {\n\t\tci.CloseIdleConnections()\n\t}\n}\n\ntype basicAuthRoundTripper struct {\n\tusername SecretReader\n\tpassword SecretReader\n\trt       http.RoundTripper\n}\n\n// NewBasicAuthRoundTripper will apply a BASIC auth authorization header to a request unless it has\n// already been set.\nfunc NewBasicAuthRoundTripper(username, password SecretReader, rt http.RoundTripper) http.RoundTripper {\n\treturn &basicAuthRoundTripper{username, password, rt}\n}\n\nfunc (rt *basicAuthRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n\tif len(req.Header.Get(\"Authorization\")) != 0 {\n\t\treturn rt.rt.RoundTrip(req)\n\t}\n\tvar username string\n\tvar password string\n\tif rt.username != nil {\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\tusername, err = rt.username.Fetch(req.Context())\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read basic auth username: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif rt.password != nil {\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\tpassword, err = rt.password.Fetch(req.Context())\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read basic auth password: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treq = cloneRequest(req)\n\treq.SetBasicAuth(username, password)\n\treturn rt.rt.RoundTrip(req)\n}\n\nfunc (rt *basicAuthRoundTripper) CloseIdleConnections() {\n\tif ci, ok := rt.rt.(closeIdler); ok {\n\t\tci.CloseIdleConnections()\n\t}\n}\n\ntype oauth2RoundTripper struct {\n\tmtx        sync.RWMutex\n\tlastRT     *oauth2.Transport\n\tlastSecret string\n\n\t// Required for interaction with Oauth2 server.\n\tconfig          *OAuth2\n\toauthCredential SecretReader\n\topts            *httpClientOptions\n\tclient          *http.Client\n}\n\nfunc NewOAuth2RoundTripper(oauthCredential SecretReader, config *OAuth2, next http.RoundTripper, opts *httpClientOptions) http.RoundTripper {\n\tif oauthCredential == nil {\n\t\toauthCredential = NewInlineSecret(\"\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn &oauth2RoundTripper{\n\t\tconfig: config,\n\t\t// A correct tokenSource will be added later on.\n\t\tlastRT:          &oauth2.Transport{Base: next},\n\t\topts:            opts,\n\t\toauthCredential: oauthCredential,\n\t}\n}\n\ntype oauth2TokenSourceConfig interface {\n\tTokenSource(ctx context.Context) oauth2.TokenSource\n}\n\nfunc (rt *oauth2RoundTripper) newOauth2TokenSource(req *http.Request, clientCredential string) (client *http.Client, source oauth2.TokenSource, err error) {\n\ttlsConfig, err := NewTLSConfig(&rt.config.TLSConfig, WithSecretManager(rt.opts.secretManager))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n\t}\n\n\ttlsTransport := func(tlsConfig *tls.Config) (http.RoundTripper, error) {\n\t\treturn &http.Transport{\n\t\t\tTLSClientConfig:       tlsConfig,\n\t\t\tProxy:                 rt.config.Proxy(),\n\t\t\tProxyConnectHeader:    rt.config.GetProxyConnectHeader(),\n\t\t\tDisableKeepAlives:     !rt.opts.keepAlivesEnabled,\n\t\t\tMaxIdleConns:          20,\n\t\t\tMaxIdleConnsPerHost:   1, // see https://github.com/golang/go/issues/13801\n\t\t\tIdleConnTimeout:       10 * time.Second,\n\t\t\tTLSHandshakeTimeout:   10 * time.Second,\n\t\t\tExpectContinueTimeout: 1 * time.Second,\n\t\t}, nil\n\t}\n\n\tvar t http.RoundTripper\n\ttlsSettings, err := rt.config.TLSConfig.roundTripperSettings(rt.opts.secretManager)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n\t}\n\tif tlsSettings.immutable() {\n\t\tt, _ = tlsTransport(tlsConfig)\n\t} else {\n\t\tt, err = NewTLSRoundTripperWithContext(req.Context(), tlsConfig, tlsSettings, tlsTransport)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif ua := req.UserAgent(); ua != \"\" {\n\t\tt = NewUserAgentRoundTripper(ua, t)\n\t}\n\n\tvar config oauth2TokenSourceConfig\n\n\tif rt.config.GrantType == grantTypeJWTBearer {\n\t\t// RFC 7523 3.1 - JWT authorization grants\n\t\t// RFC 7523 3.2 - Client Authentication Processing is not implement upstream yet,\n\t\t// see https://github.com/golang/oauth2/pull/745\n\n\t\tvar sig *jwt.SigningMethodRSA\n\t\tswitch rt.config.SignatureAlgorithm {\n\t\tcase jwt.SigningMethodRS256.Name:\n\t\t\tsig = jwt.SigningMethodRS256\n\t\tcase jwt.SigningMethodRS384.Name:\n\t\t\tsig = jwt.SigningMethodRS384\n\t\tcase jwt.SigningMethodRS512.Name:\n\t\t\tsig = jwt.SigningMethodRS512\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tsig = jwt.SigningMethodRS256\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tiss := rt.config.Iss\n\t\tif iss == \"\" {\n\t\t\tiss = rt.config.ClientID\n\t\t}\n\t\tconfig = &JwtGrantTypeConfig{\n\t\t\tPrivateKey:       []byte(clientCredential),\n\t\t\tPrivateKeyID:     rt.config.ClientCertificateKeyID,\n\t\t\tScopes:           rt.config.Scopes,\n\t\t\tTokenURL:         rt.config.TokenURL,\n\t\t\tSigningAlgorithm: sig,\n\t\t\tIss:              iss,\n\t\t\tSubject:          rt.config.ClientID,\n\t\t\tAudience:         rt.config.Audience,\n\t\t\tPrivateClaims:    rt.config.Claims,\n\t\t\tEndpointParams:   mapToValues(rt.config.EndpointParams),\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tconfig = &clientcredentials.Config{\n\t\t\tClientID:       rt.config.ClientID,\n\t\t\tClientSecret:   clientCredential,\n\t\t\tScopes:         rt.config.Scopes,\n\t\t\tTokenURL:       rt.config.TokenURL,\n\t\t\tEndpointParams: mapToValues(rt.config.EndpointParams),\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tclient = &http.Client{Transport: t}\n\tctx := context.WithValue(context.Background(), oauth2.HTTPClient, client)\n\treturn client, config.TokenSource(ctx), nil\n}\n\nfunc (rt *oauth2RoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tsecret    string\n\t\tneedsInit bool\n\t)\n\n\trt.mtx.RLock()\n\tsecret = rt.lastSecret\n\tneedsInit = rt.lastRT.Source == nil\n\trt.mtx.RUnlock()\n\n\t// Fetch the secret if it's our first run or always if the secret can change.\n\tif !rt.oauthCredential.Immutable() || needsInit {\n\t\tnewSecret, err := rt.oauthCredential.Fetch(req.Context())\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"unable to read oauth2 client secret: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif newSecret != secret || needsInit {\n\t\t\t// Secret changed or it's a first run. Rebuilt oauth2 setup.\n\t\t\tclient, source, err := rt.newOauth2TokenSource(req, newSecret)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\trt.mtx.Lock()\n\t\t\trt.lastSecret = newSecret\n\t\t\trt.lastRT.Source = source\n\t\t\tif rt.client != nil {\n\t\t\t\trt.client.CloseIdleConnections()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trt.client = client\n\t\t\trt.mtx.Unlock()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\trt.mtx.RLock()\n\tcurrentRT := rt.lastRT\n\trt.mtx.RUnlock()\n\treturn currentRT.RoundTrip(req)\n}\n\nfunc (rt *oauth2RoundTripper) CloseIdleConnections() {\n\tif rt.client != nil {\n\t\trt.client.CloseIdleConnections()\n\t}\n\tif ci, ok := rt.lastRT.Base.(closeIdler); ok {\n\t\tci.CloseIdleConnections()\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc mapToValues(m map[string]string) url.Values {\n\tv := url.Values{}\n\tfor name, value := range m {\n\t\tv.Set(name, value)\n\t}\n\n\treturn v\n}\n\n// cloneRequest returns a clone of the provided *http.Request.\n// The clone is a shallow copy of the struct and its Header map.\nfunc cloneRequest(r *http.Request) *http.Request {\n\t// Shallow copy of the struct.\n\tr2 := new(http.Request)\n\t*r2 = *r\n\t// Deep copy of the Header.\n\tr2.Header = make(http.Header)\n\tfor k, s := range r.Header {\n\t\tr2.Header[k] = s\n\t}\n\treturn r2\n}\n\ntype tlsConfigOptions struct {\n\tsecretManager SecretManager\n}\n\n// TLSConfigOption defines an option that can be applied to the HTTP client.\ntype TLSConfigOption interface {\n\tapplyToTLSConfigOptions(options *tlsConfigOptions)\n}\n\n// NewTLSConfig creates a new tls.Config from the given TLSConfig.\nfunc NewTLSConfig(cfg *TLSConfig, optFuncs ...TLSConfigOption) (*tls.Config, error) {\n\treturn NewTLSConfigWithContext(context.Background(), cfg, optFuncs...)\n}\n\n// NewTLSConfigWithContext creates a new tls.Config from the given TLSConfig.\nfunc NewTLSConfigWithContext(ctx context.Context, cfg *TLSConfig, optFuncs ...TLSConfigOption) (*tls.Config, error) {\n\topts := tlsConfigOptions{}\n\tfor _, opt := range optFuncs {\n\t\topt.applyToTLSConfigOptions(&opts)\n\t}\n\n\tif err := cfg.Validate(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\ttlsConfig := &tls.Config{\n\t\tInsecureSkipVerify: cfg.InsecureSkipVerify,\n\t\tMinVersion:         uint16(cfg.MinVersion),\n\t\tMaxVersion: It also validates that ProxyURL\n   389\u2192// is set if ProxyConnectHeader is set.\n   390\u2192func (c *HTTPClientConfig) Validate() error {\n   391\u2192\t// Backwards compatibility with the bearer_token field.\n   392\u2192\tif len(c.BearerToken) > 0 && len(c.BearerTokenFile) > 0 {\n   393\u2192\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of bearer_token & bearer_token_file must be configured\")\n   394\u2192\t}\n   395\u2192\tif (c.BasicAuth != nil || c.OAuth2 != nil) && (len(c.BearerToken) > 0 || len(c.BearerTokenFile) > 0) {\n   396\u2192\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of basic_auth, oauth2, bearer_token & bearer_token_file must be configured\")\n   397\u2192\t}\n   398\u2192\tif c.BasicAuth != nil && nonZeroCount(c.BasicAuth.Username != \"\", c.BasicAuth.UsernameFile != \"\", c.BasicAuth.UsernameRef != \"\") > 1 {\n   399\u2192\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of basic_auth username, username_file & username_ref must be configured\")\n   400\u2192\t}\n   401\u2192\tif c.BasicAuth != nil && nonZeroCount(string(c.BasicAuth.Password) != \"\", c.BasicAuth.PasswordFile != \"\", c.BasicAuth.PasswordRef != \"\") > 1 {\n   402\u2192\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of basic_auth password, password_file & password_ref must be configured\")\n   403\u2192\t}\n   404\u2192\tif c.Authorization != nil {\n   405\u2192\t\tif len(c.BearerToken) > 0 || len(c.BearerTokenFile) > 0 {\n   406\u2192\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"authorization is not compatible with bearer_token & bearer_token_file\")\n   407\u2192\t\t}\n   408\u2192\t\tif nonZeroCount(string(c.Authorization.Credentials) != \"\", c.Authorization.CredentialsFile != \"\", c.Authorization.CredentialsRef != \"\") > 1 {\n   409\u2192\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of authorization credentials & credentials_file must be configured\")\n   410\u2192\t\t}\n   411\u2192\t\tc.Authorization.Type = strings.TrimSpace(c.Authorization.Type)\n   412\u2192\t\tif len(c.Authorization.Type) == 0 {\n   413\u2192\t\t\tc.Authorization.Type = \"Bearer\"\n   414\u2192\t\t}\n   415\u2192\t\tif strings.ToLower(c.Authorization.Type) == \"basic\" {\n   416\u2192\t\t\treturn errors.New(`authorization type cannot be set to \"basic\", use \"basic_auth\" instead`)\n   417\u2192\t\t}\n   418\u2192\t\tif c.BasicAuth != nil || c.OAuth2 != nil {\n   419\u2192\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of basic_auth, oauth2 & authorization must be configured\")\n   420\u2192\t\t}\n   421\u2192\t} else {\n   422\u2192\t\tif len(c.BearerToken) > 0 {\n   423\u2192\t\t\tc.Authorization = &Authorization{Credentials: c.BearerToken}\n   424\u2192\t\t\tc.Authorization.Type = \"Bearer\"\n   425\u2192\t\t\tc.BearerToken = \"\"\n   426\u2192\t\t}\n   427\u2192\t\tif len(c.BearerTokenFile) > 0 {\n   428\u2192\t\t\tc.Authorization = &Authorization{CredentialsFile: c.BearerTokenFile}\n   429\u2192\t\t\tc.Authorization.Type = \"Bearer\"\n   430\u2192\t\t\tc.BearerTokenFile = \"\"\n   431\u2192\t\t}\n   432\u2192\t}\n   433\u2192\tif c.OAuth2 != nil {\n   434\u2192\t\tif c.BasicAuth != nil {\n   435\u2192\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of basic_auth, oauth2 & authorization must be configured\")\n   436\u2192\t\t}\n   437\u2192\t\tif len(c.OAuth2.ClientID) == 0 {\n   438\u2192\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"oauth2 client_id must be configured\")\n   439\u2192\t\t}\n   440\u2192\t\tif len(c.OAuth2.TokenURL) == 0 {\n   441\u2192\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"oauth2 token_url must be configured\")\n   442\u2192\t\t}\n   443\u2192\t\tif c.OAuth2.GrantType == grantTypeJWTBearer {\n   444\u2192\t\t\tif nonZeroCount(len(c.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKey) > 0, len(c.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKeyFile) > 0, len(c.OAuth2.ClientCertificateKeyRef) > 0) > 1 {\n   445\u2192\t\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of oauth2 client_certificate_key, client_certificate_key_file & client_certificate_key_ref must be configured using grant-type=urn:ietf:params:oauth:grant-type:jwt-bearer\")\n   446\u2192\t\t\t}\n   447\u2192\t\t\tif c.OAuth2.SignatureAlgorithm != \"\" && !slices.Contains(validSignatureAlgorithm, c.OAuth2.SignatureAlgorithm) {\n   448\u2192\t\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"valid signature algorithms are RS256, RS384 and RS512\")\n   449\u2192\t\t\t}\n   450\u2192\t\t} else if nonZeroCount(len(c.OAuth2.ClientSecret) > 0, len(c.OAuth2.ClientSecretFile) > 0, len(c.OAuth2.ClientSecretRef) > 0) > 1 {\n   451\u2192\t\t\treturn errors.New(\"at most one of oauth2 client_secret, client_secret_file & client_secret_ref must be configured using grant-type=client_credentials\")\n   452\u2192\t\t}\n   453\u2192\t}\n   454\u2192\tif err := c.ProxyConfig.Validate(); err != nil {\n   455\u2192\t\treturn err\n   456\u2192\t}\n   457\u2192\tif c.HTTPHeaders != nil {\n   458\u2192\t\tif err := c.HTTPHeaders.Validate(); err != nil {\n   459\u2192\t\t\treturn err\n   460\u2192\t\t}\n   461\u2192\t}\n   462\u2192\treturn nil\n   463\u2192}\n   464\u2192\n   465\u2192// UnmarshalYAML implements the yaml.Unmarshaler interface.\n   466\u2192func (c *HTTPClientConfig) UnmarshalYAML(unmarshal func(interface{}) error) error {\n   467\u2192\ttype plain HTTPClientConfig\n   468\u2192\t*c = DefaultHTTPClientConfig\n   469\u2192\tif err := unmarshal((*plain)(c)); err != 476\u2192func (c *HTTPClientConfig) UnmarshalJSON(data []byte) error {\n   477\u2192\ttype plain HTTPClientConfig\n   478\u2192\t*c = DefaultHTTPClientConfig\n   479\u2192\tif err := DialContextFunc func(context.Context, string, string) (net.Conn, error)\n   494\u2192\n   495\u2192// NewTLSConfigFunc returns tls.Config.\n   496\u2192type NewTLSConfigFunc func(context.Context, {\n  1303\u2192\tvar (\n  1304\u2192\t\tcertData, keyData string\n  1305\u2192\t\terr               error\n  1306\u2192\t)\n  1307\u2192\n  1308\u2192\tcertSecret, err := toSecret(secretManager,
